NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
CHANGE OF NAME
I, A. Gopi, born as an intersexed male child to Mr. P. Arasan on 7th July 1977, residing at 4-A, Valluvar Street, Serrapalli,
Rasipuram Taluk, Namakkal, after Biological Change, has been reared as a Female. (Reference: Dr. R. Rajkumar, Asst.
Professor in Urology, Government Mohankumaramangalam Medical College Hospital, Salem) The Clinical Examination
under the reference above also show that I could be reared as a Female. Hence I, A. Gopi shall henceforth be known as
A. GOPIKA.
Salem,
5th March 2010.

A. GOPI.

I, N. Prabu, born as an intersexed Male child to Mr. Natesan on 12th June 1980, residing at Perumal Koil, Near Putupatti
Main Road, Namagiripet, Namakkal, after Biological Change, has been reared as a Female. (Reference : Dr. R. Rajkumar,
Asst. Professor in Urology, Government Mohankumaramangalam Medical College Hospital, Salem) The Clinical examination
under the reference above also show that I could be reared as a Female. Hence I, N. Prabu shall henceforth be known as
N. MALAVIKA.
Namagiripet,
5th March 2010.

N. PRABU.
